#\xea\xb9\x80\xec\xb9\x98\xec\x9b\x8c\xeb\xa6\xac\xec\x96\xb4 #Kimchi #Meme #controversial #COVID-19 #Coronavirus\\\\n\\\\nSYNOPSIS:\\\\n\\\\nKIMCHI WARRIOR Returns!  Following its debut in 2010, KIMCHI WARRIOR battled illnesses throughout the ages. It\xe2\x80\x99s creator, Young Man Kang, also battled with the harsh words of netizens but through the growing world of Webfests, he fought back and is once again promoting this award-winning series in hopes that KIMCHI WARRIOR will help lift the spirits of those facing our latest foe, COVID-19, and to encourage them to join together to fight and win against this deadly global disease!\\\\n\\\\n\\\\nProduction Company:\\\\nYoung Man Kang Films \\\\nhttp:\\/\\/www.KimchiWarrior.com\\\\n\\\\nNarrator: Michael Maneage \\\\nCreator: Young Man Kang\\\\nContributing Writer: Melodie Everson \\\\n\\\\n++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++\\\\n\\\\n\\\\nAbout the Kimchi Warrior: \\\\n\\\\nThe Kimchi Warrior is a unique blend of martial arts, comedy, and the promotion of good health. Based on the premise of Popeye, our hero obtains supernatural strength by consuming the most prominent Korean dish to defend mankind from the world\'s most notorious diseases (i.e. The Swine Flu, Mad Cow Disease, Malaria, SARS etc.) Each episode a new \\\\\\"disease character\\\\\\" is summoned by Evil Lord of Disease to wipe out mankind. Under the tutelage of the clairvoyant Kimchi Master, The Kimchi Warrior is sent to fight and ultimately annihilate the disease with a different \\\\\\"ingredient weapon\\\\\\". It\'s very entertaining and educational for kids. It is also advocates good nutrition to everyone, since Kimchi is deemed one of the healthiest foods in the world.\\\\n\\\\n\\\\nEl Kimchi Warrior es una combinaci\xc3\xb3n \xc3\xbanica de artes marciales, comedia y promoci\xc3\xb3n de la buena salud. #Kimchi #Meme #controversial #COVID-19 #Coronavirus\\\\n\\\\nSYNOPSIS:\\\\n\\\\nKIMCHI WARRIOR Returns!  Following its debut in 2010, KIMCHI WARRIOR battled illnesses throughout the ages. It\xe2\x80\x99s creator, Young Man Kang, also battled with the harsh words of netizens but through the growing world of Webfests, he fought back and is once again promoting this award-winning series in hopes that KIMCHI WARRIOR will help lift the spirits of those facing our latest foe, COVID-19, and to encourage them to join together to fight and win against this deadly global disease!\\\\n\\\\n\\\\nProduction Company:\\\\nYoung Man Kang Films \\\\nhttp:\\/\\/www.KimchiWarrior.com\\\\n\\\\nNarrator: Michael Maneage \\\\nCreator: Young Man Kang\\\\nContributing Writer: Melodie Everson \\\\n\\\\n++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++\\\\n\\\\n\\\\nAbout the Kimchi Warrior: \\\\n\\\\nThe Kimchi Warrior is a unique blend of martial arts, comedy, and the promotion of good health. Based on the premise of Popeye, our hero obtains supernatural strength by consuming the most prominent Korean dish to defend mankind from the world\'s most notorious diseases (i.e. The Swine Flu, Mad Cow Disease, Malaria, SARS etc.) Each episode a new \\\\\\"disease character\\\\\\" is summoned by Evil Lord of Disease to wipe out mankind. Under the tutelage of the clairvoyant Kimchi Master, The Kimchi Warrior is sent to fight and ultimately annihilate the disease with a different \\\\\\"ingredient weapon\\\\\\". It\'s very entertaining and educational for kids. It is also advocates good nutrition to everyone, since Kimchi is deemed one of the healthiest foods in the world.\\\\n\\\\n\\\\nEl Kimchi Warrior es una combinaci\xc3\xb3n \xc3\xbanica de artes marciales, comedia y promoci\xc3\xb3n de la buena salud. Basado en la premisa de Popeye, nuestro h\xc3\xa9roe obtiene una fuerza sobrenatural al consumir el plato coreano m\xc3\xa1s destacado para defender a la humanidad de las enfermedades m\xc3\xa1s notorias del mundo (es decir, la gripe porcina, la enfermedad de las vacas locas, la malaria, el SARS, etc.) Cada episodio es una nueva \\\\\\"enfermedad personaje \\\\\\"es convocado por Evil Lord of Disease para acabar con la humanidad. Bajo la tutela del clarividente Maestro Kimchi, el Guerrero Kimchi es enviado a luchar y finalmente aniquilar la enfermedad con un \\\\\\"arma de ingredientes\\\\\\" diferente. Es muy entretenido y educativo para ni\xc3\xb1os. Tambi\xc3\xa9n aboga por una buena nutrici\xc3\xb3n para todos, ya que Kimchi es considerado uno de los alimentos m\xc3\xa1s saludables del mundo.\\\\n\\\\nCast\\\\n\\\\nKimchi Warrior -- Monir Mamoun\\\\nGochu Girl - Nora Wyman\\\\nMaster -- Tim Colceri\\\\nNarrator -- Jim Coughlin\\\\nHee Sun -- Natalee Phillips\\\\nTapas Matador -- Alexander Cukor\\\\nSalsa Matador -- J Francisco Rodriguez\\\\nCurry Warrior -- Monir Mamoun\\\\nEvil Lord of Disease -- Tim Colceri\\\\nMalaria -- Rick Phillips Jr.\\\\nMad Cow -- Jin Kelley\\\\nHee Sun Mother -- Yuka Sano\\\\nHee Sun Father -- Jae Chang\\\\nSARS -- Jim Coughlin\\\\nSwine Flu -- Jeff Ali\\\\nKid -- Nicolai Ali\\\\nIndian Kid -- Natalee Phillips\\\\n\\\\n\\\\n\\\\nCrew\\\\n\\\\nDirector -- Young Man Kang\\\\nExecutive Producer -- Jae Chang\\\\nExecutive Producer -- Seong Mook Won\\\\nStory -- Young Man Kang\\\\nWriter -- Rick Phillips Jr.\\\\nAssociate Producer - Jin Kelley\\\\nCasting Director - Jin Kelley\\\\nSound Recordist, Designer \\\\u0026 Music Composer -- Robert Hoehn\\\\nFilm Composer -- Jeff Ali\\\\nCasting Director \\\\u0026 1st AD -- Jin Kelley\\\\n2nd AD -- Hwa Kwan Eurie Sung\\\\nCreative Director -- Chan Ho Lee\\\\nAnimator -- Se Hyeong Lee\\\\nAnimator -- P. Following its debut in 2010, KIMCHI WARRIOR battled illnesses throughout the ages. It\xe2\x80\x99s creator, Young Man Kang, also battled with the harsh words of netizens but through the growing world of Webfests, he fought back and is once again promoting this award-winning series in hopes that KIMCHI WARRIOR will help lift the spirits of those facing our latest foe, COVID-19, and to encourage them to join together to fight and win against this deadly global disease!\\n\\n\\nProduction Company:\\nYoung Man Kang Films \\nhttp://www.KimchiWarrior.com\\n\\nNarrator: Michael Maneage \\nCreator: Young Man Kang\\nContributing Writer: Melodie Everson \\n\\n++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++\\n\\n\\nAbout the Kimchi Warrior: \\n\\nThe Kimchi Warrior is a unique blend of martial arts, comedy, and the promotion of good health. Based on the premise of Popeye, our hero obtains supernatural strength by consuming the most prominent Korean dish to defend mankind from the world\'s most notorious diseases (i.e. The Swine Flu, Mad Cow Disease, Malaria, SARS etc.) Each episode a new \\"disease character\\" is summoned by Evil Lord of Disease to wipe out mankind. Under the tutelage of the clairvoyant Kimchi Master, The Kimchi Warrior is sent to fight and ultimately annihilate the disease with a different \\"ingredient weapon\\". It\'s very entertaining and educational for kids. It is also advocates good nutrition to everyone, since Kimchi is deemed one of the healthiest foods in the world.\\n\\n\\nEl Kimchi Warrior es una combinaci\xc3\xb3n \xc3\xbanica de artes marciales, comedia y promoci\xc3\xb3n de la buena salud. #Coronavirus\\n\\nSYNOPSIS:\\n\\nKIMCHI WARRIOR Returns!  Following its debut in 2010, KIMCHI WARRIOR battled illnesses throughout the ages. It\xe2\x80\x99s creator, Young Man Kang, also battled with the harsh words of netizens but through the growing world of Webfests, he fought back and is once again promoting this award-winning series in hopes that KIMCHI WARRIOR will help lift the spirits of those facing our latest foe, COVID-19, and to encourage them to join together to fight and win against this deadly global disease!\\n\\n\\nProduction Company:\\nYoung Man Kang Films \\nhttp://www.KimchiWarrior.com\\n\\nNarrator: Michael Maneage \\nCreator: Young Man Kang\\nContributing Writer: Melodie Everson \\n\\n++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++++\\n\\n\\nAbout the Kimchi Warrior: \\n\\nThe Kimchi Warrior is a unique blend of martial arts, comedy, and the promotion of good health. Based on the premise of Popeye, our hero obtains supernatural strength by consuming the most prominent Korean dish to defend mankind from the world\'s most notorious diseases (i.e. The Swine Flu, Mad Cow Disease, Malaria, SARS etc.) Each episode a new \\"disease character\\" is summoned by Evil Lord of Disease to wipe out mankind. Under the tutelage of the clairvoyant Kimchi Master, The Kimchi Warrior is sent to fight and ultimately annihilate the disease with a different \\"ingredient weapon\\". It\'s very entertaining and educational for kids. It is also advocates good nutrition to everyone, since Kimchi is deemed one of the healthiest foods in the world.\\n\\n\\nEl Kimchi Warrior es una combinaci\xc3\xb3n \xc3\xbanica de artes marciales, comedia y promoci\xc3\xb3n de la buena salud. Basado en la premisa de Popeye, nuestro h\xc3\xa9roe obtiene una fuerza sobrenatural al consumir el plato coreano m\xc3\xa1s destacado para defender a la humanidad de las enfermedades m\xc3\xa1s notorias del mundo (es decir, la gripe porcina, la enfermedad de las vacas locas, la malaria, el SARS, etc.) Cada episodio es una nueva \\"enfermedad personaje \\"es convocado por Evil Lord of Disease para acabar con la humanidad. Bajo la tutela del clarividente Maestro Kimchi, el Guerrero Kimchi es enviado a luchar y finalmente aniquilar la enfermedad con un \\"arma de ingredientes\\" diferente. Es muy entretenido y educativo para ni\xc3\xb1os.
